SELECT c1."Id", c1."UpdatedAt", c1."UserId", s."Id", s."CartId", s."Quantity", s."VariantId", s."Id0", s."AvailableValues", s."IsActive", s."IsDefault", s."Price", s."ProductId", s."ReservedStockQty", s."StockQty", s."Id1", s."CategoryId", s."CreatedAt", s."Description", s."Name", s."Status", s."VendorId"
FROM (
    SELECT c."Id", c."UpdatedAt", c."UserId"
    FROM carts AS c
    WHERE c."UserId" = @userId
    LIMIT 1
) AS c1
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c0."Id", c0."CartId", c0."Quantity", c0."VariantId", p."Id" AS "Id0", p."AvailableValues", p."IsActive", p."IsDefault", p."Price", p."ProductId", p."ReservedStockQty", p."StockQty", p0."Id" AS "Id1", p0."CategoryId", p0."CreatedAt", p0."Description", p0."Name", p0."Status", p0."VendorId"
    FROM cart_items AS c0
    INNER JOIN product_variants AS p ON c0."VariantId" = p."Id"
    INNER JOIN products AS p0 ON p."ProductId" = p0."Id"
) AS s ON c1."Id" = s."CartId"
ORDER BY c1."Id", s."Id", s."Id0"
